## Interaction Log

### System — 2026-07-01T19:41:33.168740

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform comprehensive market research on **WLD‑USDT** using all available analysis tools (technical analysis, candles, order book, funding rate, news, instrument specs, portfolio assessment, position sizing, etc.). Produce a JSON response containing:
- `suggested_side` (“buy” or “sell”)
- `move_potential_pct` (estimated % price move, targeting asymmetric upside)
- `confidence` (0‑1)
- `veto` (true if any hard stop or risk factor blocks the trade)
- `thesis` (concise rationale)

**Context & Prior Findings**
- The agent previously analyzed **TAC‑USDT** (1‑hour chart) and concluded a **short bias**:
  - Price 0.040175 USDT, near lower Bollinger band, below EMA‑9/EMA‑21.
  - RSI 9.37 (deeply oversold), technical score 0.368 (bearish), short score 0.632.
  - ATR ≈ 9.7 % → supports 5‑10 % moves.
  - Support 0.038879, resistance 0.063039; suggested tight stop just below support.
- No errors occurred; all function schemas were listed but not yet invoked for WLD‑USDT.

**Open Actions Needed**
1. **Assess portfolio** to ensure no existing WLD‑USDT position or block.
2. **Get instrument specs** for WLD‑USDT (minSize, maxLeverage, etc.).
3. **Fetch latest ticker** for price reference.
4. **Run technical analysis** (EMA, RSI, ATR, Bollinger, support/resistance, scores) on appropriate timeframe (e.g., 1H).
5. **Retrieve recent candles** (e.g., 100 bars) for trend confirmation.
6. **Obtain order‑book snapshot** for liquidity and imbalance.
7. **Check funding rate** for crowding bias.
8. **Search crypto news** for WLD‑USDT (funding, sentiment, events).
9. **Compute position size** based on account equity, desired risk % (default 1 %).
10. **Ensure TP/SL** defaults are set for any new position.

**Decision Points**
- If technicals show strong asymmetric upside (e.g., price near support, bullish EMA crossover, RSI low but rising, high volatility), set `suggested_side` = “buy”.
- If bearish signals dominate, set `suggested_side` = “sell”.
- `veto` = true if:
  * Portfolio already holds WLD‑USDT (blocking new entry) or
  * Instrument minSize exceeds affordable size at target risk,
  * Funding rate is extremely adverse,
  * News indicates high macro risk (e.g., regulatory, security breach).

**Output Format Example**
```json
{
  "suggested_side": "buy",
  "move_potential_pct": 12.3,
  "confidence": 0.78,
  "veto": false,
  "thesis": "WLD‑USDT is trading near strong support with bullish EMA crossover, low RSI indicating oversold conditions, and high ATR suggesting 10‑15% upside potential; funding is neutral and news is positive."
}
```

### Key Insights for Trading Decision
- **Strong downward momentum:** Price has fallen ~9.6 % in the past 24 h, from an opening of $0.409 to $0.3698.
- **Potential volatility:** The 24‑h range (0.3598 – 0.4193) is about 16 % wide, indicating room for sizable moves.
- **Liquidity:** Order‑book depth is decent (≈ 24 k WLD on the ask side, 8 k WLD on the bid side) with a sizable 24‑h volume (~$5 M), supporting larger trades without severe slippage.
- **Current spread:** Bid‑ask spread is only $0.0001 (≈ 0.03 % of price), very tight—good for entry/exit.

### Issues / Errors
- No errors were reported; the API call returned a valid JSON payload.
- The `volCurrency24h` and `vol24h` fields have identical numeric values, which may be a data‑format quirk but does not affect the core analysis.

**Conclusion:** WLD‑USDT is experiencing a notable downtrend with high 24‑h volatility and solid liquidity, making it a candidate for a momentum‑based trade (e.g., short‑bias) if the risk‑reward profile meets the strategy’s asymmetric payoff criteria.

| **Short Score** | **0.743** (0‑1) | Strong bias toward short positions. |
| **Key Levels** | Support 0.3552 · Resistance 0.4193 · Pivot 0.3784 | Immediate support just below price; resistance far above current level. |
| **Suggested Bias** | **short** | Model recommends a short stance. |

### Key Take‑aways
- **Price is significantly under EMA9/21/50**, confirming a downtrend.
- **RSI near oversold** but still below 35, so a rebound is possible; however, other indicators (trend, momentum, technical score) stay bearish.
- **Support at ~0.3552** is close; a break below could trigger a larger move toward the next support zone.
- **Short bias (0.743)** and low technical score (0.257) suggest the symbol may be suitable for a short‑side trade, provided risk is managed (e.g., stop ~0.0095 USDT above entry).
